***пичкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пичкать.html>пи́чкать</a> (28870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, of unclear etymology, and not obviously related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pitátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to feed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пища.html>пи́ща</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">píšča</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">food</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пичкать.html>пи́чкать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">píčkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напичкать.html>напи́чкать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overfeed <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually forcibly or against someone's desires</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to overdose, to give too much medicine to (someone)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stuff, to cram (someone with useless or unnecessary knowledge or information)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to oversupply (useless or unnecessary knowledge or information)</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">запи́чкать</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapíčkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напичкать.html>напи́чкать</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">napíčkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***пища.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пища.html>пища</a> (1977)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">пишта</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pišta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*piťa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пища.html>пи́ща</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">píšča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пища.html>пи́щи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пища.html>пи́щи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пища.html>пи́щ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>food
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пища.html>пи́ща</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бого́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>píšča</b> bogóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>food</b> of the gods</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пища.html>пи́ща</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:размышление.html>размышле́ний</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>píšča</b> dlja razmyšlénij</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>food</b> for thought</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пищаль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пищаль.html>пища́ль</a> (24893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*piščalь</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пищать.html>пища́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">piščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-аль</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-alʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пищаль.html>пища́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">piščálʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пищать.html>пища́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пищать.html>пища́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пищаль.html>пища́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shepherd's pipe</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> harquebus</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hand cannon, hand bombard</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пищать.html>пища́ть</a> (16203)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pīščàti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to squeak, to whistle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пищать.html>пища́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">piščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пискнуть.html>пи́скнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to peep, to squeak <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">make a noise like a baby bird or mouse</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>First attested in 1835. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пища.html>пи́ща</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">píšča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">οἰσοφάγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oisophágos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пищевод.html>пищево́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">piščevód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пищевод.html>пищево́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пищевод.html>пищево́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пищевод.html>пищево́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gullet, oesophagus</li></ol>

***плавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:плавать.html>пла́вать</a> (2596)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*plavati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*plew-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">float</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавать.html>пла́вать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plávatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поплавать.html>попла́вать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to swim, to float</li>
<li>to sail</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is an abstract verb. Its concrete counterpart is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плыть.html>плыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<p><b>пла́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-пла-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ва</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:плавить.html>пла́вить</a> (30916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*plaviti</i>. lang="sh">пла̏вити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to float (timber), to sail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">рlаviť</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">pɫawić</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = More distantly cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавить.html>пла́вить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plávitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to melt, to fuse
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расплавить.html>распла́вить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rasplávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to smelt
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́плавить</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výplavitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to soften by heating</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to float (timber) <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to transport by floating</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавить.html>пла́вить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавиться.html>пла́виться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plávitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расплавиться.html>распла́виться</a></b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to float or swim downstream <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of timber, fish, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавник.html>плавни́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plavník</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавник.html>плавника́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавник.html>плавники́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавник.html>плавнико́в</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавный.html>пла́вный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plávnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавно.html>пла́вно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plávno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-пла́вно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)плавне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-пла́вно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)плавне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>smoothly <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a smooth manner</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Александр Солженицын, <i>Матренин <a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двор</a></i> 1968:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>пришёл</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:плавно.html>пла́вно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:повернуть.html>поверну́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:величавый.html>велича́вую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kogdá ja prišól, on <b>plávno</b> povernúl ko mne veličávuju gólovu</i></dd><dd>as I returned, he <b>smoothly</b> turned his stately head towards me</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:плавный.html>пла́вный</a> (29719)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавать.html>пла́вать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plávatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавный.html>пла́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plávnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)плавне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)плавне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>smooth, even</li>
<li>fluent, flowing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плавный.html>пла́вная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>речь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plávnaja</b> rečʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fluent speech</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>easy, light</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавный.html>пла́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plávnyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавный.html>пла́вного</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавный.html>пла́вные</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плавный.html>пла́вных</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> liquid (the consonant r or l)</li></ol>

***плакат.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:плакат.html>плака́т</a> (4629)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed in 1704 via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Plakat</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">placard</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плакат.html>плака́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plakát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плакат.html>плака́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плакат.html>плака́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плакат.html>плака́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>poster, placard, bill</li>
<li>broadsheet</li></ol>

***плакать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:плакать.html>пла́кать</a> (962)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">плакати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plakati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*plakati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плакать.html>пла́кать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plákatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заплакать.html>запла́кать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поплакать.html>попла́кать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cry, to weep</li>
<li>to mourn, to weep</li>
<li><i>in expressions</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плакать.html>пла́кали</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:денежка.html>де́нежки</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Plákali</b> dénežki!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The money has simply vanished. / You can kiss your money good-bye. / You can whistle for your money.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палка.html>па́лка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:плакать.html>пла́чет</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pálka po nemú <b>pláčet</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He's asking for it. / What he needs is a thrashing.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>хоть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:плакать.html>пла́чь</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xotʹ <b>plačʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is enough to make you weep!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плакать.html>пла́кать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жилетка.html>жиле́тку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plákatʹ</b> v žilétku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to complain, to lament</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
